#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.6.6 ③按SentinelResource资源名称限流+自定义限流返回+服务降级处理</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">按SentinelResource配置，点击超过限流配置返回自定义限流提示+程序异常返回fallback服务降级</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">微服务cloudalibaba-sentinel-service8401</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类RateLimitController</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloudalibaba.controller;

import com.alibaba.csp.sentinel.annotation.SentinelResource;
import com.alibaba.csp.sentinel.slots.block.BlockException;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

@RestController
@Slf4j
public class RateLimitController{
    @GetMapping("/rateLimit/byUrl")
    public String byUrl(){
        return "按rest地址限流测试OK";
    }

    @GetMapping("/rateLimit/byResource")
    @SentinelResource(value = "byResourceSentinelResource",blockHandler = "handleException")
    public String byResource(){
        return "按资源名称SentinelResource限流测试OK";
    }
    public String handleException(BlockException exception){
        return "服务不可用@SentinelResource启动"+"\t"+"o(╥﹏╥)o";
    }

    @GetMapping("/rateLimit/doAction/{p1}")
    @SentinelResource(value = "doActionSentinelResource",
            blockHandler = "doActionBlockHandler", fallback = "doActionFallback")
    public String doAction(@PathVariable("p1") Integer p1) {
        if (p1 == 0){
            throw new RuntimeException("p1等于零直接异常");
        }
        return "doAction";
    }

    public String doActionBlockHandler(@PathVariable("p1") Integer p1,BlockException e){
        log.error("sentinel配置自定义限流了:{}", e);
        return "sentinel配置自定义限流了";
    }

    public String doActionFallback(@PathVariable("p1") Integer p1,Throwable e){
        log.error("程序逻辑异常了:{}", e);
        return "程序逻辑异常了"+"\t"+e.getMessage();
    }

}
```

[**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/rateLimit/doAction/2</font>**](http://localhost:8401/rateLimit/doAction/2)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">配置流控规则</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">图形配置和代码关系</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888536486-cbe9fe2d-e947-416d-8622-b1b5d24b54d4.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">表示1秒钟内查询次数大于1，就跑到我们自定义的处流，限流</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">1秒钟点击1下，OK</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">超过上述，疯狂点击，返回了自己定义的限流处理信息，限流发生，配合了sentinel设定的规则</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/rateLimit/doAction/0</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">p1参数为零，异常发生，返回了自己定义的服务降级处理</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">小结</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">blockHandler，主要针对sentinel配置后出现的违规情况处理</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">fallback，程序异常了JVM抛出的异常服务降级</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">两者可以同时共存</font>

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7 热点规则</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.1 基本介绍</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">是什么</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">热点即经常访问的数据，很多时候我们希望统计或者限制某个热点数据中访问频次最高的TopN数据，并对其访问进行限流或者其它操作</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.2 官网</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">热点参数限流 · alibaba/Sentinel Wiki · GitHub</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.3 代码</font>
```java
@GetMapping("/testHotKey")
@SentinelResource(value = "testHotKey",blockHandler = "dealHandler_testHotKey")
public String testHotKey(@RequestParam(value = "p1",required = false) String p1, 
                         @RequestParam(value = "p2",required = false) String p2){
    return "------testHotKey";
}
public String dealHandler_testHotKey(String p1,String p2,BlockException exception){
    return "-----dealHandler_testHotKey";
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">sentinel系统默认的提示：Blocked by Sentinel (flow limiting) </font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.4 配置</font>
<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888536726-237913bd-1e4d-407c-9006-6e738d180beb.png)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">限流模式只支持QPS模式，固定写死了。（这才叫热点）</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">@SentinelResource注解的方法参数索引，0代表第一个参数，1代表第二个参数，以此类推</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">单机阀值以及统计窗口时长表示在此窗口时间超过阀值就限流。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上面的抓图就是第一个参数有值的话，1秒的QPS为1，超过就限流，限流后调用dealHandler_testHotKey支持方法。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">方法testHotKey里面第一个参数P1只要QPS超过每秒1次，马上降级处理</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.5 测试</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">✖</font>****<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">error</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=abc</font>](http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=abc)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">含有参数P1，当每秒访问的频率超过1次时，会触发Sentinel的限流操作</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">✖</font>****<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">error</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=abc&p2=33</font>](http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=abc&p2=33)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">含有参数P1，当每秒访问的频率超过1次时，会触发Sentinel的限流操作</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">✔</font>****<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">right</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p2=abc</font>](http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p2=abc)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">没有热点参数P1，不断访问则不会触发限流操作</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.7.6 参数例外项</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上述案例演示了第一个参数p1，当QPS超过1秒1次点击后马上被限流</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">特殊情况</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">普通正常限流</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">含有P1参数，超过1秒钟一个后，达到阈值1后马上被限流</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">例外特殊限流</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">我们期望p1参数当它是某个特殊值时，到达某个约定值后【普通正常限流】规则突然例外、失效了，它的限流值和平时不一样</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">假如当p1的值等于5时，它的阈值可以达到200或其它值</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">配置</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888536907-a48c6565-bc20-4b10-af8a-eca885be4768.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888537283-a33994f4-2ee4-48ee-bec6-740adfc608fc.png)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">添加按钮不能忘</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">测试</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">✔</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=5</font>](http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=5)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">超过1秒钟一个后，达到阈值200后才会被限流</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">当p1等于5的时候，阈值变为200</font>

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">✖</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=3</font>](http://localhost:8401/testHotKey?p1=3)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">超过1秒钟一个后，达到阈值后马上被限流</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">当p1不等于5的时候，阈值就是平常的【普通正常限流】规则</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">前提条件</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">热点参数的注意点，参数必须是基本类型或者String</font>

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.8 授权规则</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.8.1 授权规则概述</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">在某些场景下，需要根据调用接口的来源判断是否允许执行本次请求。此时就可以使用Sentinel提供的授权规则来实现，Sentinel的授权规则能够根据请求的来源判断是否允许本次请求通过。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">在Sentinel的授权规则中，提供了 白名单与黑名单 两种授权类型。白放行、黑禁止</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.8.2 官网</font>
[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">https://github.com/alibaba/Sentinel/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E7%99%BD%E5%90%8D%E5%8D%95%E6%8E%A7%E5%88%B6</font>](https://github.com/alibaba/Sentinel/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E7%99%BD%E5%90%8D%E5%8D%95%E6%8E%A7%E5%88%B6)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.8.3 演示授权规则，黑名单禁止</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">代码</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">EmpowerController</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.controller;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

@RestController
@Slf4j
public class EmpowerController //Empower授权规则，用来处理请求的来源
{
    @GetMapping(value = "/empower")
    public String requestSentinel4(){
        log.info("测试Sentinel授权规则empower");
        return "Sentinel授权规则";
    }
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">MyRequestOriginParser</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.handler;

import com.alibaba.csp.sentinel.adapter.spring.webmvc.callback.RequestOriginParser;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class MyRequestOriginParser implements RequestOriginParser{
    @Override
    public String parseOrigin(HttpServletRequest httpServletRequest) {
        return httpServletRequest.getParameter("serverName");
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">启动8401后先访问成功</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">http://localhost:8401/empower</font>](http://localhost:8401/empower)

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9 规则持久化</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.1 是什么</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">一旦我们重启微服务应用，sentinel规则将消失，生产环境需要将配置规则进行持久化</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.2 怎么玩</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">将限流配置规则持久化进Nacos保存，只要刷新8401某个rest地址，sentinel控制台的流控规则就能看到，只要Nacos里面的配置不删除，针对8401上sentinel上的流控规则持续有效</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.3 步骤</font>
##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.3.1 修改cloudalibaba-sentinel-service8401</font>
##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.3.2 POM</font>
```xml
<!--SpringCloud ailibaba sentinel-datasource-nacos -->
<dependency>
  <groupId>com.alibaba.csp</groupId>
  <artifactId>sentinel-datasource-nacos</artifactId>
</dependency>
```

##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.3.3 YML</font>
```yaml
server:
  port: 8401

spring:
  application:
    name: cloudalibaba-sentinel-service # 8401微服务提供者后续将会被纳入阿里巴巴sentinel监管
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848         # Nacos服务注册中心地址
    sentinel:
      transport:
        dashboard: localhost:8080 # 配置Sentinel dashboard控制台服务地址
        port: 8719 # 默认8719端口，假如被占用会自动从8719开始依次+1扫描,直至找到未被占用的端口
      web-context-unify: false # controller层的方法对service层调用不认为是同一个根链路
      datasource:
        ds1:  # 数据源名称
          nacos:
            server-addr: localhost:8848  # Nacos服务器地址
            dataId: ${spring.application.name}  # 使用应用名作为dataId
            groupId: DEFAULT_GROUP  # 默认分组
            data-type: json  # 规则数据格式为JSON
            rule-type: flow  # 规则类型为流控规则
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">添加Nacos数据源配置 </font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">rule-type: flow</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">备注：rule-type是什么？看看源码</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">源代码</font>**

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888537617-2cdd56b8-eee5-4633-a698-d8f7cc6424b7.png)

##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.9.3.4 添加Nacos业务规则配置</font>
<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888537660-565d0b6e-ebae-4f4e-b324-0fba06430c19.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">内容解析</font>**

```json
[
  {
    "resource": "/rateLimit/byUrl",
    "limitApp": "default",
    "grade": 1,
    "count": 1,
    "strategy": 0,
    "controlBehavior": 0,
    "clusterMode": false
  }
]
```

| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">resource：资源名称；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">limitApp：来源应用；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">grade：阈值类型，0表示线程数，1表示QPS；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">count：单机阈值；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">strategy：流控模式，0表示直接，1表示关联，2表示链路；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">controlBehavior：流控效果，0表示快速失败，1表示Warm Up，2表示排队等待；</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">clusterMode：是否集群。</font> |
| :--- |

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.10 OpenFeign和Sentinel集成实现fallback服务降级</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.10.1 需求说明</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">cloudalibaba-consumer-nacos-order83   通过OpenFeign调用    cloudalibaba-provider-payment9001</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">1 83   通过OpenFeign调用  9001微服务，正常访问OK</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2 83   通过OpenFeign调用  9001微服务，异常访问error</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">访问者要有fallback服务降级的情况，不要持续访问9001加大微服务负担，但是通过feign接口调用的各方法各自不同，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">如果每个不同方法都加一个fallback配对方法，会导致代码膨胀不好管理，工程埋雷....../(ㄒoㄒ)/~~</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3  </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">public </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">@</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">interface </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">FeignClient</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">通过fallback属性进行统一配置，feign接口里面定义的全部方法都走统一的服务降级，</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">一个搞定即可</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">4 9001微服务自身还带着sentinel内部配置的流控规则，如果满足也会被触发，也即本例有2个Case</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">4.1 OpenFeign接口的统一fallback服务降级处理</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">4.2 Sentinel访问触发了自定义的限流配置,在注解@SentinelResource里面配置的blockHandler方法。</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.10.2 程序解耦</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">前述参考</font>**

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888538433-7892fd64-f912-4c33-87d9-356a7e388849.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">本例说明</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888538603-8f86b6dd-698f-446e-be8b-ce0fff2202de.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.10.3 编码步骤</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">启动nacos服务器8848</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">startup.cmd -m standalone</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">启动Sentinel成功</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">java -jar sentinel-dashboard-1.8.6.jar</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">①修改服务提供方cloudalibaba-provider-payment9001</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">改POM</font>**

```plain
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<project xmlns="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0"
         xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
         xsi:schemaLocation="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0 http://maven.apache.org/xsd/maven-4.0.0.xsd">
    <modelVersion>4.0.0</modelVersion>
    <parent>
        <groupId>com.atguigu.cloud</groupId>
        <artifactId>mscloudV5</artifactId>
        <version>1.0-SNAPSHOT</version>
    </parent>

    <artifactId>cloudalibaba-provider-payment9001</artifactId>

    <properties>
        <maven.compiler.source>17</maven.compiler.source>
        <maven.compiler.target>17</maven.compiler.target>
        <project.build.sourceEncoding>UTF-8</project.build.sourceEncoding>
    </properties>



    <dependencies>
        <!--openfeign-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.springframework.cloud</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-cloud-starter-openfeign</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <!--alibaba-sentinel-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>com.alibaba.cloud</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-cloud-starter-alibaba-sentinel</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <!--nacos-discovery-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>com.alibaba.cloud</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-cloud-starter-alibaba-nacos-discovery</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <!-- 引入自己定义的api通用包 -->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>com.atguigu.cloud</groupId>
            <artifactId>cloud-api-commons</artifactId>
            <version>1.0-SNAPSHOT</version>
        </dependency>
        <!--SpringBoot通用依赖模块-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-web</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-actuator</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <!--hutool-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>cn.hutool</groupId>
            <artifactId>hutool-all</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <!--lombok-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.projectlombok</groupId>
            <artifactId>lombok</artifactId>
            <version>1.18.28</version>
            <scope>provided</scope>
        </dependency>
        <!--test-->
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-test</artifactId>
            <scope>test</scope>
        </dependency>
    </dependencies>

    <build>
        <plugins>
            <plugin>
                <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
                <artifactId>spring-boot-maven-plugin</artifactId>
            </plugin>
        </plugins>
    </build>

</project>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">写YML</font>**

```plain
server:
  port: 9001

spring:
  application:
    name: nacos-payment-provider
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848 #配置Nacos地址
    sentinel:
      transport:
        dashboard: localhost:8080 #配置Sentinel dashboard控制台服务地址
        port: 8719 #默认8719端口，假如被占用会自动从8719开始依次+1扫描,直至找到未被占用的端口
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">主启动</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud;

import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.jdbc.DataSourceAutoConfiguration;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.jdbc.DataSourceTransactionManagerAutoConfiguration;
import org.springframework.cloud.client.discovery.EnableDiscoveryClient;

@SpringBootApplication
@EnableDiscoveryClient
public class Main9001
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        SpringApplication.run(Main9001.class,args);
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Controller</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.controller;

import cn.hutool.core.util.IdUtil;
import com.alibaba.csp.sentinel.annotation.SentinelResource;
import com.alibaba.csp.sentinel.slots.block.BlockException;
import com.atguigu.cloud.entities.PayDTO;
import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ResultData;
import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ReturnCodeEnum;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

import java.math.BigDecimal;

@RestController
public class PayAlibabaController
{
    @Value("${server.port}")
    private String serverPort;

    @GetMapping(value = "/pay/nacos/{id}")
    public String getPayInfo(@PathVariable("id") Integer id)
    {
        return "nacos registry, serverPort: "+ serverPort+"\t id"+id;
    }

    @GetMapping("/pay/nacos/get/{orderNo}")
    @SentinelResource(value = "getPayByOrderNo",blockHandler = "handlerBlockHandler")
    public ResultData getPayByOrderNo(@PathVariable("orderNo") String orderNo)
    {
        //模拟从数据库查询出数据并赋值给DTO
        PayDTO payDTO = new PayDTO();

        payDTO.setId(1024);
        payDTO.setOrderNo(orderNo);
        payDTO.setAmount(BigDecimal.valueOf(9.9));
        payDTO.setPayNo("pay:"+IdUtil.fastUUID());
        payDTO.setUserId(1);

        return ResultData.success("查询返回值："+payDTO);
    }
    public ResultData handlerBlockHandler(@PathVariable("orderNo") String orderNo,BlockException exception)
    {
        return ResultData.fail(ReturnCodeEnum.RC500.getCode(),"getPayByOrderNo服务不可用，" +
                "触发sentinel流控配置规则"+"\t"+"o(╥﹏╥)o");
    }
    /*
    fallback服务降级方法纳入到Feign接口统一处理，全局一个
    public ResultData myFallBack(@PathVariable("orderNo") String orderNo,Throwable throwable)
    {
        return ResultData.fail(ReturnCodeEnum.RC500.getCode(),"异常情况："+throwable.getMessage());
    }
    */
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">新增PayFeignSentinelApi接口</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.apis;

import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ResultData;
import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.FeignClient;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;

@FeignClient(value = "nacos-payment-provider",fallback = PayFeignSentinelApiFallBack.class)
public interface PayFeignSentinelApi
{
    @GetMapping("/pay/nacos/get/{orderNo}")
    public ResultData getPayByOrderNo(@PathVariable("orderNo") String orderNo);
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">为远程调用新建全局统一服务降级类 fallback =PayFeignSentinelApiFallBack.class</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.apis;

import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ResultData;
import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ReturnCodeEnum;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class PayFeignSentinelApiFallBack implements PayFeignSentinelApi
{
    @Override
    public ResultData getPayByOrderNo(String orderNo)
    {
        return ResultData.fail(ReturnCodeEnum.RC500.getCode(),"对方服务宕机或不可用，FallBack服务降级o(╥﹏╥)o");
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">gav坐标</font>**

```plain

    <groupId>com.atguigu.cloud</groupId>
    <artifactId>cloud-api-commons</artifactId>
    <version>1.0-SNAPSHOT</version>
</dependency>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">主启动</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud;

import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
import org.springframework.cloud.client.discovery.EnableDiscoveryClient;
import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.EnableFeignClients;

@EnableDiscoveryClient
@SpringBootApplication
@EnableFeignClients //开启激活Feign功能
public class Main83
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        SpringApplication.run(Main83.class,args);
    }
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">添加@EnableFeignClients 启动Feign的功能</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">OrderNacosController</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.controller;

import com.atguigu.cloud.apis.PayFeignSentinelApi;
import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ResultData;
import jakarta.annotation.Resource;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
import org.springframework.web.client.RestTemplate;

@RestController
public class OrderNacosController
{
    @Resource
    private RestTemplate restTemplate;
    @Resource
    private PayFeignSentinelApi payFeignSentinelApi;

    @Value("${service-url.nacos-user-service}")
    private String serverURL;

    @GetMapping("/consumer/pay/nacos/{id}")
    public String paymentInfo(@PathVariable("id") Integer id)
    {
        String result = restTemplate.getForObject(serverURL + "/pay/nacos/" + id, String.class);
        return result+"\t"+"    我是OrderNacosController83调用者。。。。。。";
    }

    @GetMapping(value = "/consumer/pay/nacos/get/{orderNo}")
    public ResultData getPayByOrderNo(@PathVariable("orderNo") String orderNo)
    {
        return payFeignSentinelApi.getPayByOrderNo(orderNo);
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">启动83微服务，第1次</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">故障现象</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888539038-bdd259a4-dbb3-4910-856d-31cb0ab5efd3.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">导致原因</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">springboot+springcloud版本太高导致和阿里巴巴Sentinel不兼容</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">解决方案</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">总体父工程，boot+cloud降低版本</font>

| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3.2.0</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2023.0.0</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font> |
| :--- |
| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上面的配置暂时为本案例注释掉，版本降级一下。</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">讲解完后请恢复上述高版本保持前后配置一致，</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">请用下面的版本替代上述</font> |
| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3.0.9</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2022.0.2</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font> |

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888539328-2bc3d907-43b3-4ac3-acb8-1226f56cb9ac.png)

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.11 GateWay和Sentinel集成实现服务限流</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.11.1 需求说明</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">cloudalibaba-sentinel-gateway9528        保护          cloudalibaba-provider-payment9001</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.11.2 启动nacos服务器8848</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">s</font>`<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">tartup.cmd -m standalone</font>`

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.11.3 启动sentienl服务器8080</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">12.11.4 步骤</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">建Module</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">cloudalibaba-sentinel-gateway9528</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">改POM</font>**

```plain
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<project xmlns="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0"
         xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"
         xsi:schemaLocation="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0 http://maven.apache.org/xsd/maven-4.0.0.xsd">
    <parent>
        <groupId>com.atguigu.cloud</groupId>
        <artifactId>mscloudV3</artifactId>
        <version>1.0-SNAPSHOT</version>
    </parent>
    <modelVersion>4.0.0</modelVersion>

    <artifactId>cloudalibaba-sentinel-gateway9528</artifactId>

    <properties>
        <maven.compiler.source>17</maven.compiler.source>
        <maven.compiler.target>17</maven.compiler.target>
    </properties>


    <dependencies>
        <dependency>
            <groupId>org.springframework.cloud</groupId>
            <artifactId>spring-cloud-starter-gateway</artifactId>
        </dependency>
        <dependency>
            <groupId>com.alibaba.csp</groupId>
            <artifactId>sentinel-transport-simple-http</artifactId>
            <version>1.8.6</version>
        </dependency>
        <dependency>
            <groupId>com.alibaba.csp</groupId>
            <artifactId>sentinel-spring-cloud-gateway-adapter</artifactId>
            <version>1.8.6</version>
        </dependency>
        <dependency>
            <groupId>javax.annotation</groupId>
            <artifactId>javax.annotation-api</artifactId>
            <version>1.3.2</version>
            <scope>compile</scope>
        </dependency>
    </dependencies>

    <build>
        <plugins>
            <plugin>
                <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
                <artifactId>spring-boot-maven-plugin</artifactId>
            </plugin>
        </plugins>
    </build>
</project>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">写YML</font>**

```yaml
server:
  port: 9528

spring:
  application:
    name: cloudalibaba-sentinel-gateway     # sentinel+gataway整合Case
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848
    gateway:
      routes:
        - id: pay_routh1 #pay_routh1                #路由的ID(类似mysql主键ID)，没有固定规则但要求唯一，建议配合服务名
          uri: http://localhost:9001                #匹配后提供服务的路由地址
          predicates:
          - Path=/pay/**                      # 断言，路径相匹配的进行路由
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">主启动</font>**

```java
@SpringBootApplication
@EnableDiscoveryClient
public class Main9528{
    public static void main(String[] args){
        SpringApplication.run(Main9528.class,args);
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">参考官网配置说明案例改写</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888539958-3585cb42-874b-40e4-855c-c9ec431785b8.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888540189-4b84cc45-d981-46f9-8376-3605fe5f43c1.png)

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">网关限流 · alibaba/Sentinel Wiki · GitHub</font>](https://github.com/alibaba/Sentinel/wiki/%E7%BD%91%E5%85%B3%E9%99%90%E6%B5%81#spring-cloud-gateway)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">配置config</font>**

```java
/**
 * Spring Cloud Gateway  Sentinel 网关限流配置类
 * 
 * 核心功能：
 * 1. 注册 Sentinel 网关限流过滤器
 * 2. 注册 Sentinel 网关阻塞异常处理器
 * 3. 初始化网关限流规则和自定义阻塞处理器
 * 
 * 使用时只需注入对应的 SentinelGatewayFilter 实例以及 SentinelGatewayBlockExceptionHandler 实例即可
 */
@Configuration // 标识这是一个Spring配置类，用于定义Bean
public class GatewayConfiguration {

    // 视图解析器列表，用于异常处理时渲染视图（如JSON、HTML等）
    private final List<ViewResolver> viewResolvers;
    // HTTP编解码器配置，用于处理请求和响应的编解码
    private final ServerCodecConfigurer serverCodecConfigurer;

    /**
     * 构造方法，通过Spring的依赖注入机制注入所需组件
     * @param viewResolversProvider 视图解析器对象提供者（ObjectProvider提供更安全的依赖注入）
     * @param serverCodecConfigurer HTTP编解码配置器
     */
    public GatewayConfiguration(ObjectProvider<List<ViewResolver>> viewResolversProvider, 
                                ServerCodecConfigurer serverCodecConfigurer) {
        // 获取可用的视图解析器列表，如果不存在则使用空列表
        this.viewResolvers = viewResolversProvider.getIfAvailable(Collections::emptyList);
        this.serverCodecConfigurer = serverCodecConfigurer;
    }

    /**
     * 创建Sentinel网关阻塞异常处理Bean
     * 用于处理触发限流、降级等规则时的异常响应
     * 
     * @Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE) 设置最高优先级，确保此处理器最先处理异常
     * @return  Sentinel网关阻塞异常处理器
     */
    @Bean
    @Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE)
    public SentinelGatewayBlockExceptionHandler sentinelGatewayBlockExceptionHandler() {
        // 注册Sentinel网关阻塞异常处理器，用于处理Spring Cloud Gateway中的限流阻塞异常
        return new SentinelGatewayBlockExceptionHandler(viewResolvers, serverCodecConfigurer);
    }

    /**
     * 创建Sentinel网关过滤器Bean
     * 核心过滤器，用于实现网关层面的限流、降级等功能
     * 
     * @Order(-1) 设置较高优先级（Order值越小优先级越高），确保在其它过滤器之前执行
     * @return  全局过滤器实例
     */
    @Bean
    @Order(-1)
    public GlobalFilter sentinelGatewayFilter() {
        return new SentinelGatewayFilter(); // 创建Sentinel网关过滤器
    }

    /**
     * 初始化方法，在Bean创建完成后自动执行
     * 使用@PostConstruct注解标识，用于初始化网关规则和阻塞处理器
     */
    @PostConstruct // javax.annotation.PostConstruct，表示该方法在依赖注入完成后自动调用
    public void doInit() {
        // 自己动手，丰衣足食
        // initGatewayRules(); // 可以在此初始化网关规则（当前被注释）
        initBlockHandler(); // 初始化阻塞处理器（自定义限流响应）
    }

    /**
     * 初始化自定义阻塞处理器
     * 处理并自定义触发流控规则时的返回信息内容
     * 类似我们的调用触发了流控规则保护
     */
    private void initBlockHandler() {
        // 创建网关流控规则集合
        Set<GatewayFlowRule> rules = new HashSet<>();
        // 添加一条流控规则：
        // - 针对路由ID为"pay_routh1"的路由
        // - 每秒最多允许2个请求（setCount(2)）
        // - 统计时间窗口为1秒（setIntervalSec(1)）
        rules.add(new GatewayFlowRule("pay_routh1").setCount(2).setIntervalSec(1));

        // 加载流控规则到GatewayRule管理器
        GatewayRuleManager.loadRules(rules);
        
        // 创建自定义阻塞请求处理器
        BlockRequestHandler handler = new BlockRequestHandler() {
            /**
             * 处理阻塞请求的方法
             * @param exchange 服务器网络交换器，包含请求和响应信息
             * @param t 异常信息
             * @return 包装后的响应信息
             */
            @Override
            public Mono<ServerResponse> handleRequest(ServerWebExchange exchange, Throwable t) {
                // 创建返回的错误信息Map
                Map<String,String> map = new HashMap<>();
                
                // 设置错误码和错误信息
                map.put("errorCode", HttpStatus.TOO_MANY_REQUESTS.getReasonPhrase()); // "Too Many Requests"
                map.put("errorMessage", "请求太过频繁，系统忙不过来，触发限流(sentinel+gataway整合Case)");
                
                // 返回响应：
                // - 状态码：429（Too Many Requests）
                // - 内容类型：application/json
                // - 响应体：包含错误信息的Map
                return ServerResponse.status(HttpStatus.TOO_MANY_REQUESTS)
                        .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
                        .body(BodyInserters.fromValue(map));
            }
        };
        
        // 将自定义阻塞处理器设置到网关回调管理器
        GatewayCallbackManager.setBlockHandler(handler);
    }
}
```

## <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13 SpringCloud Alibaba Seata处理分布式事务</font>
<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888540482-35e37e1d-d00b-4f97-9b9f-61df83456980.png)

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.1 面试题</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.1.1 你简历上写用微服务boot/cloud做过项目，你不可能只有一个数据库吧？请你谈谈多个数据库之间你如何处理分布式事务？</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">在订单支付成功后，交易中心会调用订单中心的服务把订单状态更新，并调用物流中心的服务通知商品发货，同时还要调用积分中心的服务为用户增加相应的积分。如何保障分布式事务一致性，成为了确保订单业务稳定运行的核心诉求之一。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888540599-256429fa-8385-4e44-a74a-bd2c71945c7e.png)

#### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.1.2 我若拿出如下场景，阁下将如何应对？</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">下订单</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">冻库存</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">做支付</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">减库存</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">抵扣减：</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">积分冲抵；XX豆冲抵；礼品卷冲抵；。。。。。。</font>
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">送积分</font>**
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">做推流：</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">微信；短信；邮件；。。。。。。</font>
+ **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">派物流</font>**

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.1.3 阿里巴巴的Seata-AT模式如何做到对业务的无侵入？</font>
#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.1.4 对于分布式事务问题，你知道的解决方案有哪些?请你谈谈？</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">① 2PC（两阶段提交）</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">② 3PC（三阶段提交）</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">③ TCC方案</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">TCC(Try-Confirm-Cancel)又被称补偿事务</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">类似2PC的柔性分布式解决方案，2PC改良版</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">④ LocalMessage本地消息表；</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">⑤ 独立消息微服务+RabbitMQ/KafKa组件，实现可靠消息最终一致性方案；</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">⑥ 最大努力通知方案；</font>**

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.2 分布式事务问题如何产生？请先看业务</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上述面试问题都指向一个重要问题</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">一次业务操作需要跨多个数据源或需要跨多个系统进行远程调用，就会产生分布式事务问题</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">but</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">关系型数据库提供的能力是基于单机事务的，一旦遇到分布式事务场景，就需要通过更多其他技术手段来解决问题。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">分布式事务before</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">单机单库没这个问题</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">表结构的关系从1:1 → 1:N → N:N</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">分布式事务after</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">单体应用被拆分成微服务应用，原来的三个模块被拆分成三个独立的应用，分别使用三个独立的数据源，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务操作需要调用三个服务来完成。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">此时每个服务自己内部的数据一致性由本地事务来保证，但是全局的数据一致性问题没法保证。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888540755-2130df59-b2fe-4615-8288-4b10042c16a2.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">结论</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">迫切希望提供一种分布式事务框架，解决微服务架构下的分布式事务问题</font>

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.3 Seata简介</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">是什么</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Simple Extensible Autonomous Transaction Architecture 简单可扩展自治事务框架</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">官网解释</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888540912-36d79082-9c0e-412d-b748-f406e27d1d94.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Seata的发展历程</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">阿里巴巴作为国内最早一批进行应用分布式（微服务化）改造的企业，很早就遇到微服务架构下的分布式事务问题。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2019年1月份蚂蚁金服和阿里巴巴共同开源的分布式事务解决方案：</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2014 年，阿里中间件团队发布 TXC（Taobao Transaction Constructor），为集团内应用提供分布式事务服务。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2016 年，TXC 在经过产品化改造后，以 GTS（Global Transaction Service） 的身份登陆阿里云，成为当时业界唯一一款云上分布式事务产品。在阿云里的公有云、专有云解决方案中，开始服务于众多外部客户。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2019 年起，基于 TXC 和 GTS 的技术积累，阿里中间件团队发起了开源项目 Fescar（Fast & EaSy Commit And Rollback, FESCAR），和社区一起建设这个分布式事务解决方案。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2019 年</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> fescar(全称fast easy commit and rollback)</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> 被重命名为了seata（simple extensiable autonomous transaction architecture）。TXC、GTS、Fescar 以及 seata 一脉相承，为解决微服务架构下的分布式事务问题交出了一份与众不同的答卷。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">能干嘛</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Seata是一款开源的分布式事务解决方案，致力于在微服务架构下提供高性能和简单易用的分布式事务服务。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">去哪下</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">官网地址</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Apache Seata</font>](https://seata.io/zh-cn/index.html)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">源码地址</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Releases · apache/incubator-seata · GitHub</font>](https://github.com/seata/seata/releases)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">怎么玩</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">本地@Transactional</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">全局@GlobalTransactional</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Seata的分布式交易解决方案</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">(TC→TM→RM)分别什么意思</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888541052-688b4190-ff4e-494c-a7b0-96324f6ce92b.png)

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.4 Seata工作流程简介</font>
#### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.4.1 纵观整个分布式事务的管理，就是全局事务ID的传递和变更，要让开发者无感知</font>**
<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888541297-5b67c435-0b04-4c65-a6bb-dc585653b3f3.png)

#### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.4.2 Seata对分布式事务的协调和控制就是1+3</font>**
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">1个XID</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">XID是全局事务的唯一标识，它可以在服务的调用链路中传递，绑定到服务的事务上下文中。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">官网版3个概念(TC→TM→RM)</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888541475-12abb09f-fcb1-42a1-a27f-1654886c4cee.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">阳哥版3个概念(TC→TM→RM)</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888541518-4bc6ad81-6374-466a-bdfa-2851c06e3507.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">TC（Transaction Coordinator）事务协调器</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">就是Seata，负责维护全局事务和分支事务的状态，驱动全局事务提交或回滚。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">TM（Transaction Manager）事务管理器</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">标注全局@GlobalTransactional启动入口动作的微服务模块(比如订单模块)，它是事务的发起者，负责定义全局事务的范围，并根据TC 维护的全局事务和分支事务状态，做出开始事务、提交事务、回滚事务的决议</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">RM（Resource Manager）资源管理器</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">就是mysql数据库本身，可以是多个RM，负责管理分支事务上的资源，向 TC注册分支事务，汇报分支事务状态，驱动分支事务的提交或回滚</font>

#### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.4.3 分布式事务的执行流程-小总结</font>**
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">三个组件相互协作，TC以Seata 服务器(Server)形式独立部署，TM和RM则是以Seata Client的形式集成在微服务中运行，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">流程如下：</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">1 TM向 TC 申请开启一个全局事务，全局事务创建成功并生成一个全局唯一的 XID；</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2 XID 在微服务调用链路的上下文中传播；</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3 RM向 TC 注册分支事务，将其纳入 XID 对应全局事务的管辖；</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">4 TM 向 TC 发起针对 XID 的全局提交或回滚决议；</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">5 TC 调度 XID 下管辖的全部分支事务完成提交或回滚请求。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888541887-84887eed-e794-442b-bda1-5b7b2fb61750.png)

#### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.4.4 各事务模式</font>**
[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Seata AT 模式 | Apache Seata</font>](https://seata.io/zh-cn/docs/user/mode/at/)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">CREATE DATABASE seata;</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">USE seata;</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">在上一步seata库里建表</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">建表SQL地址</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">https://github.com/seata/seata/blob/develop/script/server/db/mysql.sql</font>](https://github.com/seata/seata/blob/develop/script/server/db/mysql.sql)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">SQL脚本内容</font>**

```sql
-- -------------------------------- The script used when storeMode is 'db' --------------------------------

-- the table to store GlobalSession data

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `global_table`

(

    `xid`                       VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,

    `transaction_id`            BIGINT,

    `status`                    TINYINT      NOT NULL,

    `application_id`            VARCHAR(32),

    `transaction_service_group` VARCHAR(32),

    `transaction_name`          VARCHAR(128),

    `timeout`                   INT,

    `begin_time`                BIGINT,

    `application_data`          VARCHAR(2000),

    `gmt_create`                DATETIME,

    `gmt_modified`              DATETIME,

    PRIMARY KEY (`xid`),

    KEY `idx_status_gmt_modified` (`status` , `gmt_modified`),

    KEY `idx_transaction_id` (`transaction_id`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB

  DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4;



-- the table to store BranchSession data

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `branch_table`

(

    `branch_id`         BIGINT       NOT NULL,

    `xid`               VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,

    `transaction_id`    BIGINT,

    `resource_group_id` VARCHAR(32),

    `resource_id`       VARCHAR(256),

    `branch_type`       VARCHAR(8),

    `status`            TINYINT,

    `client_id`         VARCHAR(64),

    `application_data`  VARCHAR(2000),

    `gmt_create`        DATETIME(6),

    `gmt_modified`      DATETIME(6),

    PRIMARY KEY (`branch_id`),

    KEY `idx_xid` (`xid`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB

  DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4;



-- the table to store lock data

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `lock_table`

(

    `row_key`        VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,

    `xid`            VARCHAR(128),

    `transaction_id` BIGINT,

    `branch_id`      BIGINT       NOT NULL,

    `resource_id`    VARCHAR(256),

    `table_name`     VARCHAR(32),

    `pk`             VARCHAR(36),

    `status`         TINYINT      NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0:locked ,1:rollbacking',

    `gmt_create`     DATETIME,

    `gmt_modified`   DATETIME,

    PRIMARY KEY (`row_key`),

    KEY `idx_status` (`status`),

    KEY `idx_branch_id` (`branch_id`),

    KEY `idx_xid` (`xid`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB

  DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4;



CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `distributed_lock`

(

    `lock_key`       CHAR(20) NOT NULL,

    `lock_value`     VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,

    `expire`         BIGINT,

    primary key (`lock_key`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB

  DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4;



INSERT INTO `distributed_lock` (lock_key, lock_value, expire) VALUES ('AsyncCommitting', ' ', 0);

INSERT INTO `distributed_lock` (lock_key, lock_value, expire) VALUES ('RetryCommitting', ' ', 0);

INSERT INTO `distributed_lock` (lock_key, lock_value, expire) VALUES ('RetryRollbacking', ' ', 0);

INSERT INTO `distributed_lock` (lock_key, lock_value, expire) VALUES ('TxTimeoutCheck', ' ', 0);
```

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6 Seata案例实战-数据库和表准备</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">订单 + 库存+ 账户</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3个业务数据库MySQL准备</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">以下演示都需要先启动Nacos后启动Seata，保证两个都OK</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6.1 分布式事务本案例业务说明</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">这里我们创建三个服务，一个订单服务，一个库存服务，一个账户服务。</font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">-------最下面还有笔记</font>_

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">当用户下单时，会在订单服务中创建一个订单，然后通过远程调用库存服务来扣减下单商品的库存，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">再通过远程调用账户服务来扣减用户账户里面的余额，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">最后在订单服务中修改订单状态为已完成。该操作跨越三个数据库，有两次远程调用，很明显会有分布式事务问题。</font>

_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">下订单 → 减库存  → 扣余额  → 改(订单)状态</font>_

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888542992-0e37cc61-933d-4ca2-8ca7-1cb4c72f1260.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888543188-b2b46060-b49a-40a5-affa-62042225abb1.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6.2 创建3个业务数据库DATABASE</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">seata_order：存储订单的数据库；</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">seata_storage：存储库存的数据库；</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">seata_account：存储账户信息的数据库。</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">建库SQL</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">CREATE DATABASE seata_order;</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">CREATE DATABASE seata_storage;</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">CREATE DATABASE seata_account;</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6.3 按照上述3库分别建对应的undo_log回滚日志表</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">订单-库存-账户3个库下都需要建各自的undo_log</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">seata官网</font>**

[<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">incubator-seata/script/client/at/db/mysql.sql at 2.x · apache/incubator-seata · GitHub</font>](https://github.com/seata/seata/blob/2.x/script/client/at/db/mysql.sql)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">undo_log建表SQL</font>**

| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">-- for AT mode you must to init this sql for you business database. the seata server not need it.</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `undo_log`</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">(</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`branch_id`     BIGINT       NOT NULL COMMENT 'branch transaction id',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`xid`           VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'global transaction id',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`context`       VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'undo_log context,such as serialization',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`rollback_info` LONGBLOB     NOT NULL COMMENT 'rollback info',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`log_status`    INT(11)      NOT NULL COMMENT '0:normal status,1:defense status',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`log_created`   DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'create datetime',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">`log_modified`  DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'modify datetime',</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">UNIQUE KEY `ux_undo_log` (`xid`, `branch_id`)</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 1 DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4 COMMENT ='AT transaction mode undo table';</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">ALTER TABLE `undo_log` ADD INDEX `ix_log_created` (`log_created`);</font> |
| :--- |


<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888543450-db81e9b8-a70e-41b0-b75e-1823ec06410e.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6.4 按照上述3库分别建对应业务表</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">t_order脚本SQL</font>**

```sql
CREATE TABLE t_order(
`id` BIGINT(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
`user_id` BIGINT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '用户id',
`product_id` BIGINT(11)DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '产品id',
`count` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '数量',
`money` DECIMAL(11,0) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '金额',
`status` INT(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '订单状态: 0:创建中; 1:已完结'
)ENGINE=INNODB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
SELECT * FROM t_order;
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">t_account脚本SQL</font>**

```sql
CREATE TABLE t_account(

`id` BIGINT(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY COMMENT 'id',

`user_id` BIGINT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '用户id',

`total` DECIMAL(10,0) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '总额度',

`used` DECIMAL(10,0) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '已用账户余额',

`residue` DECIMAL(10,0) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '剩余可用额度'

)ENGINE=INNODB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


INSERT INTO t_account(`id`,`user_id`,`total`,`used`,`residue`)VALUES('1','1','1000','0','1000');


SELECT * FROM t_account;
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">t_storage脚本SQL</font>**

```sql
CREATE TABLE t_storage(

`id` BIGINT(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

`product_id` BIGINT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '产品id',

`total` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '总库存',

`used` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '已用库存',

`residue` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '剩余库存'

)ENGINE=INNODB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


INSERT INTO t_storage(`id`,`product_id`,`total`,`used`,`residue`)VALUES('1','1','100','0','100');


SELECT * FROM t_storage;
```

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.6.5 最终All-SQL(同学们自用，同学们自用，同学们自用，)</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">建seata_order库+建t_order表+undo_log表</font>**

```sql
#order

CREATE DATABASE seata_order;

USE seata_order;

CREATE TABLE t_order(

`id` BIGINT(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

`user_id` BIGINT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '用户id',

`product_id` BIGINT(11)DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '产品id',

`count` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '数量',

`money` DECIMAL(11,0) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '金额',

`status` INT(1) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '订单状态: 0:创建中; 1:已完结'

)ENGINE=INNODB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


SELECT * FROM t_order;


-- for AT mode you must to init this sql for you business database. the seata server not need it.

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `undo_log`

(

    `branch_id`     BIGINT       NOT NULL COMMENT 'branch transaction id',

    `xid`           VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'global transaction id',

    `context`       VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'undo_log context,such as serialization',

    `rollback_info` LONGBLOB     NOT NULL COMMENT 'rollback info',

    `log_status`    INT(11)      NOT NULL COMMENT '0:normal status,1:defense status',

    `log_created`   DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'create datetime',

    `log_modified`  DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'modify datetime',

    UNIQUE KEY `ux_undo_log` (`xid`, `branch_id`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 1 DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4 COMMENT ='AT transaction mode undo table';

ALTER TABLE `undo_log` ADD INDEX `ix_log_created` (`log_created`);
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">建seata_storage库+建t_storage 表+undo_log表</font>**

```sql
#storage

CREATE DATABASE seata_storage;

USE seata_storage;

CREATE TABLE t_storage(

`id` BIGINT(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,

`product_id` BIGINT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '产品id',

`total` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '总库存',

`used` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '已用库存',

`residue` INT(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '剩余库存'

)ENGINE=INNODB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;



INSERT INTO t_storage(`id`,`product_id`,`total`,`used`,`residue`)VALUES('1','1','100','0','100');


SELECT * FROM t_storage;


 -- for AT mode you must to init this sql for you business database. the seata server not need it.

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `undo_log`

(

    `branch_id`     BIGINT       NOT NULL COMMENT 'branch transaction id',

    `xid`           VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'global transaction id',

    `context`       VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL COMMENT 'undo_log context,such as serialization',

    `rollback_info` LONGBLOB     NOT NULL COMMENT 'rollback info',

    `log_status`    INT(11)      NOT NULL COMMENT '0:normal status,1:defense status',

    `log_created`   DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'create datetime',

    `log_modified`  DATETIME(6)  NOT NULL COMMENT 'modify datetime',

    UNIQUE KEY `ux_undo_log` (`xid`, `branch_id`)

) ENGINE = InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT = 1 DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8mb4 COMMENT ='AT transaction mode undo table';

ALTER TABLE `undo_log` ADD INDEX `ix_log_created` (`log_created`);
```

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7 Seata案例实战-微服务编码落地实现</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">订单/库存/账户业务微服务Java开发准备</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.1 业务需求</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">一句话：下订单→减库存→扣余额→改（订单）状态</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">generatorConfig.xml</font>**

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE generatorConfiguration
PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD MyBatis Generator Configuration 1.0//EN"
"http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-generator-config_1_0.dtd">

<generatorConfiguration>
  <properties resource="config.properties"/>

  <context id="Mysql" targetRuntime="MyBatis3Simple" defaultModelType="flat">
    <property name="beginningDelimiter" value="`"/>
    <property name="endingDelimiter" value="`"/>

    <plugin type="tk.mybatis.mapper.generator.MapperPlugin">
      <property name="mappers" value="tk.mybatis.mapper.common.Mapper"/>
      <property name="caseSensitive" value="true"/>
    </plugin>

    <jdbcConnection driverClass="${jdbc.driverClass}"
      connectionURL="${jdbc.url}"
      userId="${jdbc.user}"
      password="${jdbc.password}">
    </jdbcConnection>

    <javaModelGenerator targetPackage="${package.name}.entities" targetProject="src/main/java"/>

    <sqlMapGenerator targetPackage="${package.name}.mapper" targetProject="src/main/java"/>

    <javaClientGenerator targetPackage="${package.name}.mapper" targetProject="src/main/java" type="XMLMAPPER"/>

    <table tableName="t_pay" domainObjectName="Pay">
      <generatedKey column="id" sqlStatement="JDBC"/>
    </table>

    <!--  seata_order -->
    <!--<table tableName="t_order" domainObjectName="Order">
    <generatedKey column="id" sqlStatement="JDBC"/>
  </table>-->

    <!--seata_storage-->
    <!--<table tableName="t_storage" domainObjectName="Storage">
    <generatedKey column="id" sqlStatement="JDBC"/>
  </table>-->

    <!--seata_account-->
    <!--<table tableName="t_account" domainObjectName="Account">
    <generatedKey column="id" sqlStatement="JDBC"/>
  </table>-->

  </context>
</generatorConfiguration>
```

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.3 修改公共cloud-api-commons新增库存和账户两个Feign服务接口</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">StorageFeignApi</font>**

```java
@FeignClient(value = "seata-storage-service")
public interface StorageFeignApi{
   //扣减库存
    @PostMapping(value = "/storage/decrease")
    ResultData decrease(@RequestParam("productId") Long productId, @RequestParam("count") Integer count);
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountFeignApi</font>**

```java
@FeignClient(value = "seata-account-service")
public interface AccountFeignApi{
    //扣减账户余额
    @PostMapping("/account/decrease")
    ResultData decrease(@RequestParam("userId") Long userId, @RequestParam("money") Long money);
}
```

##### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.4.2 改POM</font>**
```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<project xmlns="http://maven.apache.org/POM/4.0.0"
  xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"

    <version>1.0-SNAPSHOT</version>
  </parent>

  <artifactId>seata-order-service2001</artifactId>

    <maven.compiler.source>17</maven.compiler.source>
    <maven.compiler.target>17</maven.compiler.target>
    <project.build.sourceEncoding>UTF-8</project.build.sourceEncoding>
  </properties>

    <!-- nacos -->

      <groupId>com.alibaba.cloud</groupId>

            <artifactId>persistence-api</artifactId>
```

##### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.4.3 写YML</font>**
```yaml
server:
  port: 2001  # 应用服务端口号设置为2001

spring:
  application:
    name: seata-order-service  # 应用服务名称，用于服务注册与发现
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848  # Nacos服务注册中心地址
  
  # 数据源配置（使用Druid连接池和MySQL 8驱动）
  datasource:
    type: com.alibaba.druid.pool.DruidDataSource  # 使用阿里巴巴Druid连接池
    driver-class-name: com.mysql.cj.jdbc.Driver   # MySQL 8.x驱动
    # 数据库连接URL，包含字符编码、SSL、时区等参数配置
    url: jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/seata_order?characterEncoding=utf8&useSSL=false&serverTimezone=GMT%2B8&rewriteBatchedStatements=true&allowPublicKeyRetrieval=true
    username: root      # 数据库用户名
    password: 123456    # 数据库密码

# MyBatis配置
mybatis:
  mapper-locations: classpath:mapper/*.xml  # MyBatis映射文件位置
  type-aliases-package: com.atguigu.cloud.entities  # 实体类别名包路径
  configuration:
    map-underscore-to-camel-case: true  # 开启数据库下划线命名到Java驼峰命名的自动映射

# Seata分布式事务配置
seata:
  registry:
    type: nacos  # 使用Nacos作为注册中心
    nacos:
      server-addr: 127.0.0.1:8848  # Nacos服务器地址
      namespace: ""                # 命名空间，空表示使用public命名空间
      group: SEATA_GROUP           # Seata分组
      application: seata-server    # Seata服务端应用名
  tx-service-group: default_tx_group  # 事务组名称，用于获取TC服务集群名称
  service:
    vgroup-mapping:                # 事务组与TC服务集群的映射关系
      default_tx_group: default    # 将default_tx_group映射到default集群
  data-source-proxy-mode: AT       # 使用AT模式（自动事务模式）

# 日志配置
logging:
  level:
    io:
      seata: info  # 设置Seata相关日志级别为info
```

```yaml
#seata:
#  registry: # seata注册配置
#    type: nacos # seata注册类型
#    nacos:
#      application: seata-server #seata应用名称
#      server-addr: 127.0.0.1:8848
#      namespace: ""
#      group: SEATA_GROUP
#      cluster: default
#  config:             # seata配置抓取
#    nacos:
#      server-addr: 127.0.0.1:8848
#      namespace: ""
#      group: SEATA_GROUP
#      username: nacos
#      password: nacos
#  tx-service-group: default_tx_group # 事务组，由它获得TC服务的集群名称
#  service:
#    vgroup-mapping:
#      default_tx_group: default # 事务群组的映射配置关系
#  data-source-proxy-mode: AT
#  application-id: seata-server
```

##### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.4.4 主启动</font>**
```java
/**
 * Seata订单服务主应用类
 * 端口: 2001
 * 功能: 订单服务的分布式事务管理
 */
@SpringBootApplication
@MapperScan("com.atguigu.cloud.mapper") // MyBatis mapper接口扫描
@EnableDiscoveryClient // 启用服务注册与发现功能
@EnableFeignClients // 启用Feign客户端进行服务间调用
public class SeataOrderMainApp2001 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        SpringApplication.run(SeataOrderMainApp2001.class, args);
    }
}
```

##### **<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.4.5 业务类</font>**
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">entities</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Order</font>

```java
@Table(name = "t_order")
@ToString
public class Order implements Serializable
{
    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(generator = "JDBC")
    private Long id;

    /**
     * 用户id
     */
    @Column(name = "user_id")
    private Long userId;

    /**
     * 产品id
     */
    @Column(name = "product_id")
    private Long productId;

    /**
     * 数量
     */
    private Integer count;

    /**
     * 金额
     */
    private Long money;

    /**
     * 订单状态：0：创建中；1：已完结
     */
    private Integer status;

    /**
     * @return id
     */
    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    /**
     * @param id
     */
    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    /**
     * 获取用户id
     *
     * @return user_id - 用户id
     */
    public Long getUserId() {
        return userId;
    }

    /**
     * 设置用户id
     *
     * @param userId 用户id
     */
    public void setUserId(Long userId) {
        this.userId = userId;
    }

    /**
     * 获取产品id
     *
     * @return product_id - 产品id
     */
    public Long getProductId() {
        return productId;
    }

    /**
     * 设置产品id
     *
     * @param productId 产品id
     */
    public void setProductId(Long productId) {
        this.productId = productId;
    }

    /**
     * 获取数量
     *
     * @return count - 数量
     */
    public Integer getCount() {
        return count;
    }

    /**
     * 设置数量
     *
     * @param count 数量
     */
    public void setCount(Integer count) {
        this.count = count;
    }

    /**
     * 获取金额
     *
     * @return money - 金额
     */
    public Long getMoney() {
        return money;
    }

    /**
     * 设置金额
     *
     * @param money 金额
     */
    public void setMoney(Long money) {
        this.money = money;
    }

    /**
     * 获取订单状态：0：创建中；1：已完结
     *
     * @return status - 订单状态：0：创建中；1：已完结
     */
    public Integer getStatus() {
        return status;
    }

    /**
     * 设置订单状态：0：创建中；1：已完结
     *
     * @param status 订单状态：0：创建中；1：已完结
     */
    public void setStatus(Integer status) {
        this.status = status;
    }
}
```

```java
public interface OrderMapper extends Mapper<Order> {
}
```

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN" "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.atguigu.cloud.mapper.OrderMapper">
  <resultMap id="BaseResultMap" type="com.atguigu.cloud.entities.Order">
    <!--
    WARNING - @mbg.generated
    -->
    <id column="id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="id" />
    <result column="user_id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="userId" />
    <result column="product_id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="productId" />
    <result column="count" jdbcType="INTEGER" property="count" />
    <result column="money" jdbcType="DECIMAL" property="money" />
    <result column="status" jdbcType="INTEGER" property="status" />
  </resultMap>

</mapper>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Service接口及实现</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">OrderService</font>

```java
void create(Order order);
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">OrderServiceImpl</font>

```java
/**
 * 下订单->减库存->扣余额->改(订单)状态
 */
@Slf4j
@Service
public class OrderServiceImpl implements OrderService
{
    @Resource
    private OrderMapper orderMapper;
    @Resource//订单微服务通过OpenFeign去调用库存微服务
    private StorageFeignApi storageFeignApi;
    @Resource//订单微服务通过OpenFeign去调用账户微服务
    private AccountFeignApi accountFeignApi;


    @Override
    @GlobalTransactional(name = "zzyy-create-order",rollbackFor = Exception.class) //AT
    //@GlobalTransactional @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class) //XA
    public void create(Order order) {

        //xid全局事务id的检查，重要
        String xid = RootContext.getXID();

        //1. 新建订单
        log.info("==================>开始新建订单"+"\t"+"xid_order:" +xid);
        //订单状态status：0：创建中；1：已完结
        order.setStatus(0);
        int result = orderMapper.insertSelective(order);

        //插入订单成功后获得插入mysql的实体对象
        Order orderFromDB = null;
        if(result > 0)
        {
            orderFromDB = orderMapper.selectOne(order);
            //orderFromDB = orderMapper.selectByPrimaryKey(order.getId());
            log.info("-------> 新建订单成功，orderFromDB info: "+orderFromDB);
            System.out.println();
            //2. 扣减库存
            log.info("-------> 订单微服务开始调用Storage库存，做扣减count");
            storageFeignApi.decrease(orderFromDB.getProductId(), orderFromDB.getCount());
            log.info("-------> 订单微服务结束调用Storage库存，做扣减完成");
            System.out.println();
            //3. 扣减账号余额
            log.info("-------> 订单微服务开始调用Account账号，做扣减money");
            accountFeignApi.decrease(orderFromDB.getUserId(), orderFromDB.getMoney());
            log.info("-------> 订单微服务结束调用Account账号，做扣减完成");
            System.out.println();
            //4. 修改订单状态
            //订单状态status：0：创建中；1：已完结
            log.info("-------> 修改订单状态");
            orderFromDB.setStatus(1);

            Example whereCondition=new Example(Order.class);
            Example.Criteria criteria=whereCondition.createCriteria();
            criteria.andEqualTo("userId",orderFromDB.getUserId());
            criteria.andEqualTo("status",0);

            int updateResult = orderMapper.updateByExampleSelective(orderFromDB, whereCondition);

            log.info("-------> 修改订单状态完成"+"\t"+updateResult);
            log.info("-------> orderFromDB info: "+orderFromDB);
        }
        System.out.println();
        log.info("==================>结束新建订单"+"\t"+"xid_order:" +xid);

    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Controller</font>**

```java
@RestController
public class OrderController {
    @Resource
    private OrderService orderService;
    //创建订单
    @GetMapping("/order/create")
    public ResultData create(Order order){
        orderService.create(order);
        return ResultData.success(order);
    }
}
```

##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.5.3 </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">写YML</font>**
```yaml
server:
  port: 2002  # 库存服务端口号为2002，与订单服务(2001)区分

spring:
  application:
    name: seata-storage-service  # 服务名称改为库存服务
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848  # Nacos服务注册中心地址
  
  # 数据源配置 - 连接到不同的数据库
  datasource:
    type: com.alibaba.druid.pool.DruidDataSource
    driver-class-name: com.mysql.cj.jdbc.Driver
    # 注意：这里连接的是seata_storage数据库，不是seata_order
    url: jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/seata_storage?characterEncoding=utf8&useSSL=false&serverTimezone=GMT%2B8&rewriteBatchedStatements=true&allowPublicKeyRetrieval=true
    username: root
    password: 123456

# MyBatis配置
mybatis:
  mapper-locations: classpath:mapper/*.xml
  type-aliases-package: com.atguigu.cloud.entities
  configuration:
    map-underscore-to-camel-case: true

# Seata配置 - 与订单服务保持一致
seata:
  registry:
    type: nacos
    nacos:
      server-addr: 127.0.0.1:8848
      namespace: ""
      group: SEATA_GROUP
      application: seata-server
  tx-service-group: default_tx_group  # 使用相同的事务组，确保在同一个分布式事务中
  service:
    vgroup-mapping:
      default_tx_group: default  # 映射到相同的TC集群
  data-source-proxy-mode: AT  # 使用AT模式

# 日志配置
logging:
  level:
    io:
      seata: info
```

##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.5.5 </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类</font>**
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">entities</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Storage</font>

```java
@Table(name = "t_storage")
public class Storage implements Serializable
{
    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(generator = "JDBC")
    private Long id;

    /**
     * 产品id
     */
    @Column(name = "product_id")
    private Long productId;

    /**
     * 总库存
     */
    private Integer total;

    /**
     * 已用库存
     */
    private Integer used;

    /**
     * 剩余库存
     */
    private Integer residue;

    /**
     * @return id
     */
    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    /**
     * @param id
     */
    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    /**
     * 获取产品id
     *
     * @return product_id - 产品id
     */
    public Long getProductId() {
        return productId;
    }

    /**
     * 设置产品id
     *
     * @param productId 产品id
     */
    public void setProductId(Long productId) {
        this.productId = productId;
    }

    /**
     * 获取总库存
     *
     * @return total - 总库存
     */
    public Integer getTotal() {
        return total;
    }

    /**
     * 设置总库存
     *
     * @param total 总库存
     */
    public void setTotal(Integer total) {
        this.total = total;
    }

    /**
     * 获取已用库存
     *
     * @return used - 已用库存
     */
    public Integer getUsed() {
        return used;
    }

    /**
     * 设置已用库存
     *
     * @param used 已用库存
     */
    public void setUsed(Integer used) {
        this.used = used;
    }

    /**
     * 获取剩余库存
     *
     * @return residue - 剩余库存
     */
    public Integer getResidue() {
        return residue;
    }

    /**
     * 设置剩余库存
     *
     * @param residue 剩余库存
     */
    public void setResidue(Integer residue) {
        this.residue = residue;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString()
    {
        return "Storage{" +
                "id=" + id +
                ", productId=" + productId +
                ", total=" + total +
                ", used=" + used +
                ", residue=" + residue +
                '}';
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">StorageMapper</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">StorageMapper接口</font>

```java
public interface StorageMapper extends Mapper<Storage>{
    /**
     * 扣减库存
     */
    void decrease(@Param("productId") Long productId, @Param("count") Integer count);

}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">resources文件夹下新建mapper文件夹后添加StorageMapper.xml</font>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN" "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.atguigu.cloud.mapper.StorageMapper">
  <resultMap id="BaseResultMap" type="com.atguigu.cloud.entities.Storage">
    <!--
    WARNING - @mbg.generated
    -->
    <id column="id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="id" />
    <result column="product_id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="productId" />
    <result column="total" jdbcType="INTEGER" property="total" />
    <result column="used" jdbcType="INTEGER" property="used" />
    <result column="residue" jdbcType="INTEGER" property="residue" />
  </resultMap>

  <update id="decrease">
    UPDATE
    t_storage
    SET
    used = used + #{count},
    residue = residue - #{count}
    WHERE product_id = #{productId}
  </update>

</mapper>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Service接口及实现</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">StorageService</font>

```java
public interface StorageService {
    /**
     * 扣减库存
     */
    void decrease(Long productId, Integer count);
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">StorageServiceImpl</font>

```java
@Service
@Slf4j
public class StorageServiceImpl implements StorageService{
    @Resource
    private StorageMapper storageMapper;
    //扣减库存
    @Override
    public void decrease(Long productId, Integer count) {
        log.info("------->storage-service中扣减库存开始");
        storageMapper.decrease(productId,count);
        log.info("------->storage-service中扣减库存结束");
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Controller</font>**

```java
@RestController
public class StorageController{
    @Resource
    private StorageService storageService;
    //扣减库存
    @RequestMapping("/storage/decrease")
    public ResultData decrease(Long productId, Integer count) {
        storageService.decrease(productId, count);
        return ResultData.success("扣减库存成功!");
    }
}
```
