##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.6.3 </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">写YML</font>**
```plain
server:
  port: 2003

spring:
  application:
    name: seata-account-service
  cloud:
    nacos:
      discovery:
        server-addr: localhost:8848         #Nacos服务注册中心地址
  # ==========applicationName + druid-mysql8 driver===================
  datasource:
    type: com.alibaba.druid.pool.DruidDataSource
    driver-class-name: com.mysql.cj.jdbc.Driver
    url: jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/seata_account?characterEncoding=utf8&useSSL=false&serverTimezone=GMT%2B8&rewriteBatchedStatements=true&allowPublicKeyRetrieval=true
    username: root
    password: 123456
# ========================mybatis===================
mybatis:
  mapper-locations: classpath:mapper/*.xml
  type-aliases-package: com.atguigu.cloud.entities
  configuration:
    map-underscore-to-camel-case: true



# ========================seata===================
seata:
  registry:
    type: nacos
    nacos:
      server-addr: 127.0.0.1:8848
      namespace: ""
      group: SEATA_GROUP
      application: seata-server
  tx-service-group: default_tx_group # 事务组，由它获得TC服务的集群名称
  service:
    vgroup-mapping:
      default_tx_group: default # 事务组与TC服务集群的映射关系
  data-source-proxy-mode: AT

logging:
  level:
    io:
      seata: info
```

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud;

import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;
import org.springframework.cloud.client.discovery.EnableDiscoveryClient;
import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.EnableFeignClients;
import tk.mybatis.spring.annotation.MapperScan;

@EnableDiscoveryClient
@EnableFeignClients
@MapperScan("com.atguigu.cloud.mapper") //import tk.mybatis.spring.annotation.MapperScan;
@SpringBootApplication
public class SeataAccountMainApp2003{
    public static void main(String[] args){
        SpringApplication.run(SeataAccountMainApp2003.class,args);
    }
}
```

##### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.7.6.5 </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">业务类</font>**
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">entities</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Account</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.entities;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.GeneratedValue;
import javax.persistence.Id;
import javax.persistence.Table;
import java.io.Serializable;


@Table(name = "t_account")
public class Account implements Serializable
{
    /**
     * id
     */
    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(generator = "JDBC")
    private Long id;

    /**
     * 用户id
     */
    @Column(name = "user_id")
    private Long userId;

    /**
     * 总额度
     */
    private Long total;

    /**
     * 已用余额
     */
    private Long used;

    /**
     * 剩余可用额度
     */
    private Long residue;

    /**
     * 获取id
     *
     * @return id - id
     */
    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    /**
     * 设置id
     *
     * @param id id
     */
    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    /**
     * 获取用户id
     *
     * @return user_id - 用户id
     */
    public Long getUserId() {
        return userId;
    }

    /**
     * 设置用户id
     *
     * @param userId 用户id
     */
    public void setUserId(Long userId) {
        this.userId = userId;
    }

    /**
     * 获取总额度
     *
     * @return total - 总额度
     */
    public Long getTotal() {
        return total;
    }

    /**
     * 设置总额度
     *
     * @param total 总额度
     */
    public void setTotal(Long total) {
        this.total = total;
    }

    /**
     * 获取已用余额
     *
     * @return used - 已用余额
     */
    public Long getUsed() {
        return used;
    }

    /**
     * 设置已用余额
     *
     * @param used 已用余额
     */
    public void setUsed(Long used) {
        this.used = used;
    }

    /**
     * 获取剩余可用额度
     *
     * @return residue - 剩余可用额度
     */
    public Long getResidue() {
        return residue;
    }

    /**
     * 设置剩余可用额度
     *
     * @param residue 剩余可用额度
     */
    public void setResidue(Long residue) {
        this.residue = residue;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString()
    {
        return "Account{" +
                "id=" + id +
                ", userId=" + userId +
                ", total=" + total +
                ", used=" + used +
                ", residue=" + residue +
                '}';
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountMapper</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountMapper接口</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.mapper;

import com.atguigu.cloud.entities.Account;
import org.apache.ibatis.annotations.Param;
import tk.mybatis.mapper.common.Mapper;

public interface AccountMapper extends Mapper<Account>{

    /**
     * @param userId
     * @param money 本次消费金额
     */
    void decrease(@Param("userId") Long userId, @Param("money") Long money);
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">resources文件夹下新建mapper文件夹后添加AccountMapper.xml</font>

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<!DOCTYPE mapper PUBLIC "-//mybatis.org//DTD Mapper 3.0//EN" "http://mybatis.org/dtd/mybatis-3-mapper.dtd">
<mapper namespace="com.atguigu.cloud.mapper.AccountMapper">
  <resultMap id="BaseResultMap" type="com.atguigu.cloud.entities.Account">
    <!--
    WARNING - @mbg.generated
    -->
    <id column="id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="id" />
    <result column="user_id" jdbcType="BIGINT" property="userId" />
    <result column="total" jdbcType="DECIMAL" property="total" />
    <result column="used" jdbcType="DECIMAL" property="used" />
    <result column="residue" jdbcType="DECIMAL" property="residue" />
  </resultMap>

  <!--
  money   本次消费金额

  t_account数据库表
  total总额度 = 累计已消费金额(used) + 剩余可用额度(residue)
  -->
  <update id="decrease">
    UPDATE
    t_account
    SET
    residue = residue - #{money},used = used + #{money}
    WHERE user_id = #{userId};
  </update>

</mapper>
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Service接口及实现</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountService</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.service;

import org.apache.ibatis.annotations.Param;

public interface AccountService {

    /**
     * 扣减账户余额
     * @param userId 用户id
     * @param money 本次消费金额
     */
    void decrease(@Param("userId") Long userId, @Param("money") Long money);
}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountServiceImpl</font>

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.service.impl;

import com.atguigu.cloud.mapper.AccountMapper;
import com.atguigu.cloud.service.AccountService;
import jakarta.annotation.Resource;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

@Service
@Slf4j
public class AccountServiceImpl implements AccountService{
    @Resource
    AccountMapper accountMapper;

    /**
     * 扣减账户余额
     */
    @Override
    public void decrease(Long userId, Long money) {
        log.info("------->account-service中扣减账户余额开始");
        accountMapper.decrease(userId,money);
        //myTimeOut();
        //int age = 10/0;
        log.info("------->account-service中扣减账户余额结束");
    }

    /**
     * 模拟超时异常，全局事务回滚
     */
    private static void myTimeOut(){
        try { TimeUnit.SECONDS.sleep(65); } catch (InterruptedException e) { e.printStackTrace(); }
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">Controller</font>**

```java
package com.atguigu.cloud.controller;

import com.atguigu.cloud.resp.ResultData;
import com.atguigu.cloud.service.AccountService;
import jakarta.annotation.Resource;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestParam;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

@RestController
public class AccountController {

    @Resource
    AccountService accountService;
    /**
     * 扣减账户余额
     */
    @RequestMapping("/account/decrease")
    public ResultData decrease(@RequestParam("userId") Long userId, @RequestParam("money") Long money){
        accountService.decrease(userId,money);
        return ResultData.success("扣减账户余额成功！");
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">导致原因</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">springboot+springcloud版本太高导致和阿里巴巴Seata不兼容</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">解决方案</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">总体父工程，boot+cloud降低版本</font>

| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3.2.0</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2023.0.0</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font> |
| :--- |
| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上面的配置暂时为本案例注释掉，版本降级一下。</font><br/><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">讲解完后请恢复上述高版本保持前后配置一致，</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">请用下面的任一个版本替代上述</font> |
| <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3.0.9</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2022.0.2</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font> |
| _<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><!--</font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">仅为了整合</font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">openfeign + alibaba seata</font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">的案例，降低版本处理下</font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"> </font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">--></font>_<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3.1.7</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.boot.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">   </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"><</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2022.0.4</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);"></</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">spring.cloud.version</font>**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">></font> |

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.8.4 超时异常出错，没有@GlobalTransactional</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">修改seata-account-service2003微服务，AccountServiceImpl添加超时</font>**

```java
@Service
@Slf4j
public class AccountServiceImpl implements AccountService{
    @Resource
    AccountMapper accountMapper;

    /**
     * 扣减账户余额
     */
    @Override
    public void decrease(Long userId, Long money) {
        log.info("------->account-service中扣减账户余额开始");
        accountMapper.decrease(userId,money);
        myTimeOut();//服务超时
        //int age = 10/0;
        log.info("------->account-service中扣减账户余额结束");
    }
    /**
     * 模拟超时异常，全局事务回滚
     */
    private static void myTimeOut()
    {
        try { TimeUnit.SECONDS.sleep(65); } catch (InterruptedException e) { e.printStackTrace(); }
    }
}
```

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">故障情况</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">当库存和账户金额扣减后，订单状态并没有设置为已经完成，没有从零改为1</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">数据库情况</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888546187-e0de125c-4e1a-4833-b584-0ae73b9ca2ad.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888546203-7a063ca1-9721-4dc4-9002-5743d6f900d6.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888546333-f06e1712-7cbf-47b0-b0b6-1859e74652c8.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.8.5 超时异常解决，添加@GlobalTransactional</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AccountServiceImpl保留超时方法</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">OrderServiceImpl@GlobalTransactional</font>**

```java
@Override
@GlobalTransactional(name = "zzyy-create-order",rollbackFor = Exception.class) //AT
public void create(Order order){

    。。。。。。

}
```

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">此时，订单模块就是TM，也是其中一个RM</font>

![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888546982-e1fd3375-8a92-401b-8edd-4f7389f1f6c8.png)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">按照正常逻辑，本该有新记录入库，等待最后完成提交。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">回滚后</font>**

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">order记录都添加不进来</font>**

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888547448-3aded4bf-94d7-425c-a293-c4ca2e744884.png)

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">上一步准备新增的记录被彻底回滚了，保证的一致性。</font>

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">全部回退</font>**

### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.9 Seata原理小总结和面试题</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">AT模式如何做到对业务的无侵入</font>

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.9.1 是什么</font>
<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888547357-55afd170-91b2-424a-a9ed-5816c9e2439d.png)

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888547410-89adf35f-a170-4e2e-8343-f41990634a04.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.9.2 一阶段加载</font>
<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">在一阶段，Seata 会拦截“业务 SQL”，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">1  解析 SQL 语义，找到“业务 SQL”要更新的业务数据，在业务数据被更新前，将其保存成“before image”，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">2  执行“业务 SQL”更新业务数据，在业务数据更新之后，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">3  其保存成“after image”，最后生成行锁。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">以上操作全部在一个数据库事务内完成，这样保证了一阶段操作的原子性。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888547833-f032da5e-f7bc-4dd6-a8f2-ba5c80317209.png)

#### <font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">13.9.3 二阶段分2种情况</font>
**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">正常提交</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">二阶段如是顺利提交的话，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">因为“业务 SQL”在一阶段已经提交至数据库，所以Seata框架只需将一阶段保存的快照数据和行锁删掉，完成数据清理即可。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888547961-ba73c799-2acd-4c21-8400-f7dd1c31b7d4.png)

**<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">异常回滚</font>**

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">二阶段回滚：</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">二阶段如果是回滚的话，Seata 就需要回滚一阶段已经执行的“业务 SQL”，还原业务数据。</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">回滚方式便是用“before image”还原业务数据；但在还原前要首先要校验脏写，对比“数据库当前业务数据”和 “after image”，</font>

<font style="background-color:rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);">如果两份数据完全一致就说明没有脏写，可以还原业务数据，如果不一致就说明有脏写，出现脏写就需要转人工处理。</font>

<!-- 这是一张图片，ocr 内容为： -->
![](https://cdn.nlark.com/yuque/0/2025/png/58546395/1756888548344-068aa717-0d6c-4294-9b0d-d62db397368c.png)
